[  164s]                                     var animalSnifferSignaturesArtifactId = &quot;java13-sun&quot;;
[  164s] 
[  164s]                                     var felixJavaVersion = System.getProperty(&quot;felix.java.version&quot;);
[  164s]                                     if (!felixJavaVersion) {
[  164s]                                         felixJavaVersion = project.getProperty(&quot;felix.java.version&quot;);
[  164s]                                     }
[  164s] 
[  164s]                                     if (felixJavaVersion == &quot;4&quot;) {
[  164s]                                         animalSnifferSignaturesArtifactId = &quot;java14-sun&quot;;
[  164s]                                     } else if (felixJavaVersion == &quot;5&quot;) {
[  164s]                                         animalSnifferSignaturesArtifactId = &quot;java15&quot;;
[  164s]                                     } else if (felixJavaVersion == &quot;6&quot;) {
[  164s]                                         animalSnifferSignaturesArtifactId = &quot;java16&quot;;
[  164s] 										animalSnifferSignaturesVersion = &quot;1.1&quot;;
[  164s]                                     } else if (felixJavaVersion == &quot;7&quot;) {
[  164s]                                         animalSnifferSignaturesArtifactId = &quot;java17&quot;;
[  164s] 	                                } else if ( felixJavaVersion == &quot;8&quot;) {
[  164s]                                         // there are no published signatures for Java 1.8, so skip execution. However, we also need a valid
[  164s]                                         // artifact in the signature, so fallback to the 1.7 signatures and skip checking entirely
[  164s]                                         // see also https://github.com/mojohaus/animal-sniffer/issues/1
[  164s]                                         animalSnifferSignaturesArtifactId = &quot;java17&quot;;
[  164s] 	                                    skipAnimalSniffer = true;
[  164s] 	                                } else if ( felixJavaVersion != &quot;3&quot;) {
[  164s]                                         System.out.println(&quot;Unsupported felix.java.version=&quot; + felixJavaVersion + &quot;; must be 3, 4, 5, 6, 7 or 8.&quot;);
[  164s]                                         throw &quot;felix.java.version must be 3, 4, 5, 6, 7 or 8&quot;;
[  164s]                                     }
[  164s] 	                                System.out.println(&quot;Using felix.java.version=&quot; + felixJavaVersion);
[  164s]                                     project.setProperty(&quot;felix.bree&quot;, &quot;JavaSE-1.&quot; + felixJavaVersion);
[  164s]                                     project.setProperty(&quot;felix.animal.sniffer.skip&quot;, skipAnimalSniffer);
[  164s]                                     project.setProperty(&quot;felix.java.signature.version&quot;, animalSnifferSignaturesVersion);
[  164s]                                     project.setProperty(&quot;felix.java.signature.artifactId&quot;, animalSnifferSignaturesArtifactId);</script>
[  164s]   </target>
[  164s]   <testSourceRoot>${testSourceRoot}</testSourceRoot>
[  164s]   <versionsPropertyName default-value="maven.project.dependencies.versions"/>
[  164s] </configuration>
